Personal information that we collect and disclose

During the last 12 months, we've collected and disclosed the following types of personal information for one or more business purposes:
  • Identifiers
  • Characteristics of protected classifications under California or federal law
  • Commercial information
  • Internet or other electronic network activity information
  • Geolocation data
  • Electronic, visual, or similar information, such as your profile picture or photos
  • Professional or employment-related information
  • Inferences we draw from personal information
  • Other information you provide, such as your bio, Pins, messages, and comments
    • '
We have collected personal information about you from the following sources in the last 12 months:
  • You/Your device
  • Our partners, advertisers, and other third parties
How we used and shared your data in the last 12 months

We use your information to do the following:
  • Provide the Pinterest services
  • Communicate with you to provide updates or respond to your comments and questions
  • Audit our service
  • Detect and prevent security breaches and fraud
  • Fix errors and bugs
  • Maintain your account
  • Provide customer service
  • Process or fulfill orders
  • Research and development
  • Show advertisements and measure the effectiveness of Pinterest advertising
  • Market our services
  • Understand how users interact with our service
We may have shared your personal information with the following third parties in the last 12 months:
  • Advertisers
  • ISPs
  • Analytics Providers
  • OS/Platform Provider
  • Social Networks, at your direction
  • Resellers
  • Affiliates
  • Vendors
  • Legal authorities or others as necessary to comply with a law, regulation, or legal request
  • Other third parties if we are legally required, in a merger or acquisition, or with your permission
Please see your personalized report for access to your specific pieces of information we have collected from or about you or your device in the last 12 months.
